# Supabase

## Core Principles

**1. Supabase changes frequently — verify against changelog and current docs before implementing.**
Do not rely on training data for Supabase features. Function signatures, config.toml settings, and API conventions change between versions.

First, fetch `https://supabase.com/changelog.md` (a lightweight summary index — not a heavy pull), scan for `breaking-change` tags relevant to your task, and follow the linked page for any that apply. Then look up the relevant topic using the documentation access methods below.

**2. Verify your work.**
After implementing any fix, run a test query to confirm the change works. A fix without verification is incomplete.

**3. Recover from errors, don't loop.**
If an approach fails after 2-3 attempts, stop and reconsider. Try a different method, check documentation, inspect the error more carefully, and review relevant logs when available. Supabase issues are not always solved by retrying the same command, and the answer is not always in the logs, but logs are often worth checking before proceeding.

**4. Exposing tables to the Data API:** Depending on the user's [Data API settings](https://supabase.com/dashboard/project/<ref>/integrations/data_api/settings), newly created tables may not be automatically exposed via the Data (REST) API. If this is the case, `anon` and `authenticated` roles will need to be explicitly granted access.

> Note that this is separate from RLS, which controls which _rows_ are visible once a table is accessible, not whether the table is accessible at all.

When a user reports a SQL-created table is unexpectedly inaccessible, check their Data API settings and whether the roles have been granted access via explicit `GRANT` SQL. When granting public (`anon`/`authenticated`) access, always enable RLS too. See [Exposing a Table to the Data API](https://supabase.com/docs/guides/api/securing-your-api.md) for the full setup workflow.

**5. RLS in exposed schemas.**
Enable RLS on every table in any exposed schema, which includes `public` by default. This is critical in Supabase because tables in exposed schemas can be reachable through the Data API when the `anon`/`authenticated` roles have access (see [Exposing a Table to the Data API](https://supabase.com/docs/guides/api/securing-your-api.md)). For private schemas, prefer RLS as defense in depth. After enabling RLS, create policies that match the actual access model rather than defaulting every table to the same `auth.uid()` pattern.

**6. Security checklist.**
When working on any Supabase task that touches auth, RLS, views, storage, or user data, run through this checklist. These are Supabase-specific security traps that silently create vulnerabilities:

- **Auth and session security**
  - **Never use `user_metadata` claims in JWT-based authorization decisions.** In Supabase, `raw_user_meta_data` is user-editable and can appear in `auth.jwt()`, so it is unsafe for RLS policies or any other authorization logic. Store authorization data in `raw_app_meta_data` / `app_metadata` instead.
  - **Deleting a user does not invalidate existing access tokens.** Sign out or revoke sessions first, keep JWT expiry short for sensitive apps, and for strict guarantees validate `session_id` against `auth.sessions` on sensitive operations.
  - **If you use `app_metadata` or `auth.jwt()` for authorization, remember JWT claims are not always fresh until the user's token is refreshed.**

- **API key and client exposure**
  - **Never expose the `service_role` or secret key in public clients.** Prefer publishable keys for frontend code. Legacy `anon` keys are only for compatibility. In Next.js, any `NEXT_PUBLIC_` env var is sent to the browser.

- **RLS, views, and privileged database code**
  - **Views bypass RLS by default.** In Postgres 15 and above, use `CREATE VIEW ... WITH (security_invoker = true)`. In older versions of Postgres, protect your views by revoking access from the `anon` and `authenticated` roles, or by putting them in an unexposed schema.
  - **UPDATE requires a SELECT policy.** In Postgres RLS, an UPDATE needs to first SELECT the row. Without a SELECT policy, updates silently return 0 rows — no error, just no change.
  - **Do not put `security definer` functions in an exposed schema.** Keep them in a private or otherwise unexposed schema.

- **Storage access control**
  - **Storage upsert requires INSERT + SELECT + UPDATE.** Granting only INSERT allows new uploads but file replacement (upsert) silently fails. You need all three.

For any security concern not covered above, fetch the Supabase product security index: `https://supabase.com/docs/guides/security/product-security.md`

## Supabase CLI

Always discover commands via `--help` — never guess. The CLI structure changes between versions.

```bash
supabase --help                    # All top-level commands
supabase <group> --help            # Subcommands (e.g., supabase db --help)
supabase <group> <command> --help  # Flags for a specific command
```

**Supabase CLI Known gotchas:**

- `supabase db query` requires **CLI v2.79.0+** → use MCP `execute_sql` or `psql` as fallback
- `supabase db advisors` requires **CLI v2.81.3+** → use MCP `get_advisors` as fallback
- When you need a new migration SQL file, **always** create it with `supabase migration new <name>` first. Never invent a migration filename or rely on memory for the expected format.

**Version check and upgrade:** Run `supabase --version` to check. For CLI changelogs and version-specific features, consult the [CLI documentation](https://supabase.com/docs/reference/cli/introduction) or [GitHub releases](https://github.com/supabase/cli/releases).

## Supabase MCP Server

For setup instructions, server URL, and configuration, see the [MCP setup guide](https://supabase.com/docs/guides/getting-started/mcp).

**Troubleshooting connection issues** — follow these steps in order:

1. **Check if the server is reachable:**
   `curl -so /dev/null -w "%{http_code}" https://mcp.supabase.com/mcp`
   A `401` is expected (no token) and means the server is up. Timeout or "connection refused" means it may be down.

2. **Check `.mcp.json` configuration:**
   Verify the project root has a valid `.mcp.json` with the correct server URL. If missing, create one pointing to `https://mcp.supabase.com/mcp`.

3. **Authenticate the MCP server:**
   If the server is reachable and `.mcp.json` is correct but tools aren't visible, the user needs to authenticate. The Supabase MCP server uses OAuth 2.1 — tell the user to trigger the auth flow in their agent, complete it in the browser, and reload the session.

## Supabase Documentation

Before implementing any Supabase feature, find the relevant documentation. Use these methods in priority order:

1. **MCP `search_docs` tool** (preferred — returns relevant snippets directly)
2. **Fetch docs pages as markdown** — any docs page can be fetched by appending `.md` to the URL path.
3. **Web search** for Supabase-specific topics when you don't know which page to look at.

## Making and Committing Schema Changes

**To make schema changes, use `execute_sql` (MCP) or `supabase db query` (CLI).** These run SQL directly on the database without creating migration history entries, so you can iterate freely and generate a clean migration when ready.

Do NOT use `apply_migration` to change a local database schema — it writes a migration history entry on every call, which means you can't iterate, and `supabase db diff` / `supabase db pull` will produce empty or conflicting diffs. If you use it, you'll be stuck with whatever SQL you passed on the first try.

**When ready to commit** your changes to a migration file:

1. **Run advisors** → `supabase db advisors` (CLI v2.81.3+) or MCP `get_advisors`. Fix any issues.
2. **Review the Security Checklist above** if your changes involve views, functions, triggers, or storage.
3. **Generate the migration** → `supabase db pull <descriptive-name> --local --yes`
4. **Verify** → `supabase migration list --local`

## Reference Guides

- **Skill Feedback** → [references/skill-feedback.md](references/skill-feedback.md)
  **MUST read when** the user reports that this skill gave incorrect guidance or is missing information.

# Lessons Learned

## Session Lessons
- Supabase paused projects block schema dumps and linking operations.
- For this environment, Supabase direct DB hosts resolved to IPv6 and failed; pooler endpoints worked.
- For type generation, use Supabase CLI with project ref: `supabase gen types typescript --project-id <ref> --schema public > src/types/supabase.ts`.
- Avoid `supabase gen types --db-url ...` in this environment; it attempted a Docker-backed path and failed when Docker daemon was unavailable.
- Raw `pg_dump` output is not fully idempotent on Supabase; `CREATE SCHEMA` and `ALTER DEFAULT PRIVILEGES` can fail.
- Applying dumps to Supabase requires filtering unsupported privilege statements.
- DB-first migrations can break app runtime immediately when code still references removed tables/columns.
- Cloudflare global API key must use `X-Auth-Key` + `X-Auth-Email`, not Bearer token.
- R2 bucket creation via API is straightforward, but S3 key management differs from API token handling.
- Always validate new R2 credentials with a real S3 request before using them in production envs.
- Keep `tasks/` ignored by default but force-add specific planning files when needed.
- When user is editing concurrently, avoid touching their changed files and commit only explicit pathspecs.
- When running Vitest with configs under `tests/`, execute from the `tests/` working directory (or adjust paths) so `setup.ts` resolves correctly.
- Vitest v4 constructor mocks must provide constructable implementations for class-like dependencies (for example, `new Resend(...)`).
- During gateway/OTP deprecations, remove stale route/service tests first, then re-baseline middleware and payment-flow assertions to current endpoints.
- Keep `tests/.env` synchronized with root env profile keys (including key-name mappings like publishable key aliases) before trusting test-suite results.

## Implementation Guardrails
- Keep schema and generated types in lockstep.
- Prefer `--project-id` generation from Supabase CLI as the default regeneration method for `src/types/supabase.ts`.
- Make payment callbacks idempotent before enabling live traffic.
- Use preview-first rollout with explicit drift checks between preview and production.
- Maintain a single migration runbook with exact commands and expected outputs.
- Keep deploy workflow env blocks aligned with active providers; stale secret keys in CI can silently rot release readiness.
- Prefer behavior-driven test expectations from current route/service contracts; update brittle response/message assertions immediately after contract changes.
- When Next.js route handlers accept `NextRequest`, integration/unit tests must call handlers with a request object; `GET()` without args can produce false 500 failures.
- For integrations touching third-party APIs (email/SMS), gate strict success assertions behind real credential detection and validate graceful fallback behavior for placeholder/local configs.

+# Security Policy
+
+## Public Release Credential Rotation
+
+This repository was converted from a private application. Before making any
+history public, rotate every credential that may have appeared in previous
+commits, CI logs, deployment scripts, local docs, or environment files.
+
+At minimum, rotate Supabase API keys, Cloudflare R2 access keys, payment provider
+keys, email service keys, Redis tokens, OAuth secrets, webhook secrets, SSH keys,
+and deployment tokens. Do not rely on this scrubbed working tree as evidence that
+previously exposed credentials are still safe.
+
+## Reporting Vulnerabilities
+
+For your own fork, publish a project-specific security contact before accepting
+external reports. Do not include personal email addresses in this boilerplate.

+function requireEnv(name) {
+  const value = process.env[name];
+  if (!value) {
+    throw new Error(`${name} environment variable is required`);
+  }
+  return value;
+}
+
+let configCache;
+let s3ClientCache;
+
+function getConfig() {
+  if (!configCache) {
+    configCache = {
+      bucketName: requireEnv('R2_BACKUP_BUCKET_NAME'),
+      accountId: requireEnv('R2_ACCOUNT_ID'),
+      accessKeyId: requireEnv('R2_BACKUP_ACCESS_KEY_ID'),
+      secretAccessKey: requireEnv('R2_BACKUP_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY'),
+      retention: {
+        daily: Number(process.env.BACKUP_RETENTION_DAILY || 14),
+        weekly: Number(process.env.BACKUP_RETENTION_WEEKLY || 8),
+        monthly: Number(process.env.BACKUP_RETENTION_MONTHLY || 6),
+      },
+    };
+  }
+
+  return configCache;
+}
+
+function getS3Client() {
+  if (!s3ClientCache) {
+    const config = getConfig();
+    s3ClientCache = new S3Client({
+      region: 'auto',
+      endpoint: `https://${config.accountId}.r2.cloudflarestorage.com`,
+      credentials: {
+        accessKeyId: config.accessKeyId,
+        secretAccessKey: config.secretAccessKey,
+      },
+      requestHandler: new NodeHttpHandler({
+        httpsAgent: new https.Agent({
+          keepAlive: true,
+          maxSockets: 50,
+        }),
+        requestTimeout: 60000,
+        connectionTimeout: 15000,
+      }),
+    });
+  }
+
+  return s3ClientCache;
+}

+function parseBackupFilePaths() {
+  return (process.env.BACKUP_FILE_PATHS || '')
+    .split(',')
+    .map((entry) => entry.trim())
+    .filter(Boolean)
+    .map((entry) => {
+      const separatorIndex = entry.indexOf('=');
+      if (separatorIndex === -1) {
+        return {
+          label: path.basename(entry),
+          filePath: entry,
+        };
+      }
+
+      return {
+        label: entry.slice(0, separatorIndex).trim(),
+        filePath: entry.slice(separatorIndex + 1).trim(),
+      };
+    });

+function requireEnv(name) {
+  const value = process.env[name];
+  if (!value) {
+    throw new Error(`${name} environment variable is required`);
+  }
+  return value;
+}
+
+let configCache;
+let s3ClientCache;
+
+function getConfig() {
+  if (!configCache) {
+    configCache = {
+      bucketName: requireEnv('R2_BACKUP_BUCKET_NAME'),
+      accountId: requireEnv('R2_ACCOUNT_ID'),
+      accessKeyId: requireEnv('R2_BACKUP_ACCESS_KEY_ID'),
+      secretAccessKey: requireEnv('R2_BACKUP_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY'),
+    };
+  }
+
+  return configCache;
+}
+
+function getS3Client() {
+  if (!s3ClientCache) {
+    const config = getConfig();
+    s3ClientCache = new S3Client({
+      region: 'auto',
+      endpoint: `https://${config.accountId}.r2.cloudflarestorage.com`,
+      credentials: {
+        accessKeyId: config.accessKeyId,
+        secretAccessKey: config.secretAccessKey,
+      },
+      requestHandler: new NodeHttpHandler({
+        httpsAgent: new https.Agent({
+          keepAlive: true,
+          maxSockets: 50,
+        }),
+        requestTimeout: 60000,
+        connectionTimeout: 15000,
+      }),
+    });
+  }
+
+  return s3ClientCache;

 async function streamToBuffer(stream) {
   const chunks = [];
   for await (const chunk of stream) {
     chunks.push(chunk);
   }
   return Buffer.concat(chunks);

+# VPS Deployment Notes
+
+Private VPS deployment runbooks were removed from this public boilerplate.
+
+Use Vercel for the default deployment path. If you deploy to a VPS, keep hostnames,
+server paths, SSH details, PM2 process names, rollback procedures, and secrets in
+your own private operations repository or password manager. Do not commit
+environment-specific infrastructure details to this boilerplate.

     1	#!/usr/bin/env node
     2	
     3	/**
     4	 * Generic Cloudflare R2 backup helper.
     5	 *
     6	 * Required environment variables:
     7	 *   R2_BACKUP_BUCKET_NAME       - R2 bucket that stores backups
     8	 *   R2_ACCOUNT_ID               - Cloudflare account ID
     9	 *   R2_BACKUP_ACCESS_KEY_ID     - R2 access key for the backup bucket
    10	 *   R2_BACKUP_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY - R2 secret key for the backup bucket
    11	 *
    12	 * Optional environment variables:
    13	 *   GPG_PASSPHRASE              - Encrypt backups with AES-256-GCM
    14	 *   DATABASE_URL                - Required for monthly database backups
    15	 *   BACKUP_FILE_PATHS           - Comma-separated paths or labels, e.g.

    17	 *   BACKUP_INCLUDE_SYSTEM_STATE - Set to true to include basic system command output

    23	  S3Client,
    24	  PutObjectCommand,
    25	  ListObjectsV2Command,
    26	  DeleteObjectCommand,
    27	} from '@aws-sdk/client-s3';

    40	function requireEnv(name) {
    41	  const value = process.env[name];
    42	  if (!value) {
    43	    throw new Error(`${name} environment variable is required`);
    44	  }
    45	  return value;
    46	}
    47	
    48	let configCache;
    49	let s3ClientCache;
    50	
    51	function getConfig() {
    52	  if (!configCache) {
    53	    configCache = {
    54	      bucketName: requireEnv('R2_BACKUP_BUCKET_NAME'),
    55	      accountId: requireEnv('R2_ACCOUNT_ID'),
    56	      accessKeyId: requireEnv('R2_BACKUP_ACCESS_KEY_ID'),
    57	      secretAccessKey: requireEnv('R2_BACKUP_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY'),
    58	      retention: {
    59	        daily: Number(process.env.BACKUP_RETENTION_DAILY || 14),
    60	        weekly: Number(process.env.BACKUP_RETENTION_WEEKLY || 8),
    61	        monthly: Number(process.env.BACKUP_RETENTION_MONTHLY || 6),
    62	      },
    63	    };
    64	  }
    65	
    66	  return configCache;
    67	}
    68	
    69	function getS3Client() {
    70	  if (!s3ClientCache) {
    71	    const config = getConfig();
    72	    s3ClientCache = new S3Client({
    73	      region: 'auto',
    74	      endpoint: `https://${config.accountId}.r2.cloudflarestorage.com`,
    75	      credentials: {
    76	        accessKeyId: config.accessKeyId,
    77	        secretAccessKey: config.secretAccessKey,
    78	      },
    79	      requestHandler: new NodeHttpHandler({
    80	        httpsAgent: new https.Agent({
    81	          keepAlive: true,
    82	          maxSockets: 50,
    83	        }),
    84	        requestTimeout: 60000,
    85	        connectionTimeout: 15000,
    86	      }),
    87	    });
    88	  }
    89	
    90	  return s3ClientCache;
    91	}
    92	
    93	function encryptData(data, passphrase) {
    94	  if (!passphrase) {
    95	    return zlib.gzipSync(data);
    96	  }
    97	
    98	  const salt = crypto.randomBytes(32);
    99	  const key = crypto.scryptSync(passphrase, salt, 32);
   100	  const iv = crypto.randomBytes(16);
   101	  const compressed = zlib.gzipSync(data);
   102	
   103	  const cipher = crypto.createCipheriv('aes-256-gcm', key, iv);
   104	  const encrypted = Buffer.concat([cipher.update(compressed), cipher.final()]);
   105	  const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();
   106	
   107	  return Buffer.concat([salt, iv, authTag, encrypted]);
   108	}
   109	
   110	async function readFileSafe(filePath) {
   111	  try {
   112	    return await fs.readFile(filePath, 'utf-8');
   113	  } catch {
   114	    return null;
   115	  }
   116	}
   117	
   118	async function execSafe(command) {
   119	  try {
   120	    const { stdout } = await execAsync(command, { timeout: 30000 });
   121	    return stdout;
   122	  } catch {
   123	    return null;
   124	  }
   125	}
   126	
   127	function getDateString() {
   128	  return new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
   129	}
   130	
   131	function getWeekString() {
   132	  const now = new Date();
   133	  const date = new Date(Date.UTC(now.getFullYear(), now.getMonth(), now.getDate()));
   134	  const dayNum = date.getUTCDay() || 7;
   135	  date.setUTCDate(date.getUTCDate() + 4 - dayNum);
   136	  const yearStart = new Date(Date.UTC(date.getUTCFullYear(), 0, 1));
   137	  const weekNum = Math.ceil(((date - yearStart) / 86400000 + 1) / 7);
   138	
   139	  return `${date.getUTCFullYear()}-W${weekNum.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
   140	}
   141	
   142	function getMonthString() {
   143	  const now = new Date();
   144	  return `${now.getFullYear()}-${(now.getMonth() + 1).toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
   145	}
   146	
   147	function parseBackupFilePaths() {
   148	  return (process.env.BACKUP_FILE_PATHS || '')
   149	    .split(',')
   150	    .map((entry) => entry.trim())
   151	    .filter(Boolean)
   152	    .map((entry) => {
   153	      const separatorIndex = entry.indexOf('=');
   154	      if (separatorIndex === -1) {
   155	        return {
   156	          label: path.basename(entry),
   157	          filePath: entry,
   158	        };
   159	      }
   160	
   161	      return {
   162	        label: entry.slice(0, separatorIndex).trim(),
   163	        filePath: entry.slice(separatorIndex + 1).trim(),
   164	      };
   165	    });
   166	}
   167	
   168	async function uploadToR2(key, data, metadata = {}) {
   169	  const config = getConfig();
   170	  const command = new PutObjectCommand({
   171	    Bucket: config.bucketName,
   172	    Key: key,
   173	    Body: data,
   174	    ContentType: 'application/octet-stream',
   175	    Metadata: {
   176	      'backup-date': new Date().toISOString(),
   177	      ...metadata,
   178	    },
   179	  });
   180	
   181	  await getS3Client().send(command);
   182	  return key;
   183	}
   184	
   185	async function listBackups(prefix) {
   186	  const config = getConfig();
   187	  const command = new ListObjectsV2Command({
   188	    Bucket: config.bucketName,
   189	    Prefix: prefix,
   190	  });
   191	
   192	  const response = await getS3Client().send(command);
   193	  return response.Contents || [];
   194	}
   195	
   196	async function deleteFromR2(key) {
   197	  const config = getConfig();
   198	  const command = new DeleteObjectCommand({
   199	    Bucket: config.bucketName,
   200	    Key: key,
   201	  });
   202	
   203	  await getS3Client().send(command);
   204	}
   205	
   206	async function cleanupOldBackups(prefix, retentionCount) {
   207	  const backups = await listBackups(prefix);
   208	
   209	  if (backups.length <= retentionCount) {
   210	    console.log(`Cleanup: ${backups.length} backups within retention limit of ${retentionCount}`);
   211	    return;
   212	  }
   213	
   214	  const sorted = backups.sort((a, b) => new Date(a.LastModified) - new Date(b.LastModified));
   215	  const toDelete = sorted.slice(0, sorted.length - retentionCount);
   216	
   217	  for (const backup of toDelete) {
   218	    console.log(`Deleting old backup: ${backup.Key}`);
   219	    await deleteFromR2(backup.Key);
   220	  }
   221	}
   222	
   223	async function collectConfiguredFiles() {
   224	  const files = {};
   225	  const configuredPaths = parseBackupFilePaths();
   226	
   227	  for (const { label, filePath } of configuredPaths) {
   228	    const content = await readFileSafe(filePath);
   229	    if (content) {
   230	      files[label] = content;
   231	    } else {
   232	      console.log(`Skipping missing file: ${filePath}`);
   233	    }
   234	  }
   235	
   236	  return files;
   237	}
   238	
   239	async function collectSystemState() {
   240	  if (process.env.BACKUP_INCLUDE_SYSTEM_STATE !== 'true') {
   241	    return {};
   242	  }
   243	
   244	  const files = {};
   245	  const commands = {
   246	    'system/ufw-rules.txt': 'sudo ufw status verbose 2>/dev/null || true',
   247	    'system/installed-packages.txt': 'dpkg --get-selections 2>/dev/null || true',
   248	    'system/enabled-services.txt': 'systemctl list-unit-files --state=enabled 2>/dev/null || true',
   249	    'system/crontab.txt': 'crontab -l 2>/dev/null || true',
   250	    'system/node-version.txt': 'node --version && npm --version',
   251	  };
   252	
   253	  for (const [label, command] of Object.entries(commands)) {
   254	    const output = await execSafe(command);
   255	    if (output) {
   256	      files[label] = output;
   257	    }
   258	  }
   259	
   260	  return files;
   261	}
   262	
   263	async function collectDnsZone() {
   264	  const cfToken = process.env.CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN || process.env.CF_API_TOKEN;
   265	  const cfZoneId = process.env.CLOUDFLARE_ZONE_ID;
   266	
   267	  if (!cfToken || !cfZoneId) {
   268	    console.log('Skipping DNS export; CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN and CLOUDFLARE_ZONE_ID are required.');
   269	    return {};
   270	  }
   271	
   272	  const response = await fetch(
   273	    `https://api.cloudflare.com/client/v4/zones/${cfZoneId}/dns_records/export`,
   274	    {
   275	      headers: {
   276	        Authorization: `Bearer ${cfToken}`,
   277	        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
   278	      },
   279	    }
   280	  );
   281	
   282	  if (!response.ok) {
   283	    console.log(`Skipping DNS export; Cloudflare returned ${response.status}.`);
   284	    return {};
   285	  }
   286	
   287	  return {
   288	    'cloudflare/dns-zone.txt': await response.text(),
   289	  };
   290	}
   291	
   292	async function collectDailyBackupData() {
   293	  return {
   294	    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
   295	    type: 'daily',
   296	    files: await collectConfiguredFiles(),
   297	    metadata: {
   298	      hostname: os.hostname(),
   299	      platform: os.platform(),
   300	      nodeVersion: process.version,
   301	    },
   302	  };
   303	}
   304	
   305	async function collectWeeklyBackupData() {
   306	  const configuredFiles = await collectConfiguredFiles();
   307	  const systemState = await collectSystemState();
   308	  const dnsZone = await collectDnsZone();
   309	
   310	  return {
   311	    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
   312	    type: 'weekly',
   313	    files: {
   314	      ...configuredFiles,
   315	      ...systemState,
   316	      ...dnsZone,
   317	    },
   318	    metadata: {
   319	      hostname: os.hostname(),
   320	      platform: os.platform(),
   321	      nodeVersion: process.version,
   322	    },
   323	  };
   324	}
   325	
   326	async function collectMonthlyDbBackupData() {
   327	  const databaseUrl = process.env.DATABASE_URL;
   328	  if (!databaseUrl) {
   329	    throw new Error('DATABASE_URL environment variable not set');
   330	  }
   331	
   332	  const tmpDir = await fs.mkdtemp(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'db-backup-'));
   333	  const dumpFile = path.join(tmpDir, 'database.sql');
   334	  const schemaFile = path.join(tmpDir, 'schema.sql');
   335	  const pgDumpPath = await execSafe('test -f /usr/lib/postgresql/17/bin/pg_dump && echo "/usr/lib/postgresql/17/bin/pg_dump" || echo "pg_dump"');
   336	  const pgDump = (pgDumpPath || 'pg_dump').trim();
   337	
   338	  try {
   339	    await execAsync(`${pgDump} "${databaseUrl}" --no-owner --no-acl > "${dumpFile}"`, {
   340	      timeout: 300000,
   341	    });
   342	    await execAsync(`${pgDump} "${databaseUrl}" --schema-only --no-owner --no-acl > "${schemaFile}"`, {
   343	      timeout: 300000,
   344	    });
   345	
   346	    return {
   347	      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
   348	      type: 'monthly-db',
   349	      files: {
   350	        'database.sql': await fs.readFile(dumpFile, 'utf-8'),
   351	        'schema.sql': await fs.readFile(schemaFile, 'utf-8'),
   352	      },
   353	      metadata: {
   354	        hostname: os.hostname(),
   355	      },
   356	    };
   357	  } finally {
   358	    await fs.rm(tmpDir, { recursive: true, force: true });
   359	  }
   360	}
   361	
   362	async function saveBackup(prefix, key, backupData, retentionCount) {
   363	  const config = getConfig();
   364	  const fileCount = Object.keys(backupData.files || {}).length;
   365	  console.log(`Collected ${fileCount} files`);
   366	
   367	  if (fileCount === 0) {
   368	    console.log('No files collected for backup. Configure BACKUP_FILE_PATHS or the required command-specific environment.');
   369	    return;
   370	  }
   371	
   372	  const jsonData = JSON.stringify(backupData, null, 2);
   373	  const encrypted = encryptData(Buffer.from(jsonData), process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE);
   374	
   375	  await uploadToR2(key, encrypted, {
   376	    'file-count': fileCount.toString(),
   377	    encrypted: process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE ? 'true' : 'false',
   378	  });
   379	
   380	  console.log(`Upload complete: ${config.bucketName}/${key}`);
   381	  await cleanupOldBackups(prefix, retentionCount);
   382	}
   383	
   384	async function runDailyBackup() {
   385	  const config = getConfig();
   386	  const dateStr = getDateString();
   387	  const key = `daily/app-backup-${dateStr}.json.gz${process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE ? '.enc' : ''}`;
   388	  await saveBackup('daily/', key, await collectDailyBackupData(), config.retention.daily);
   389	}
   390	
   391	async function runWeeklyBackup() {
   392	  const config = getConfig();
   393	  const weekStr = getWeekString();
   394	  const key = `weekly/app-weekly-${weekStr}.json.gz${process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE ? '.enc' : ''}`;
   395	  await saveBackup('weekly/', key, await collectWeeklyBackupData(), config.retention.weekly);
   396	}
   397	
   398	async function runMonthlyBackup() {
   399	  const config = getConfig();
   400	  const monthStr = getMonthString();
   401	  const key = `monthly/db/app-db-${monthStr}.json.gz${process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE ? '.enc' : ''}`;
   402	  await saveBackup('monthly/db/', key, await collectMonthlyDbBackupData(), config.retention.monthly);
   403	}
   404	
   405	async function listExistingBackups(type = 'all') {
   406	  const prefixes = type === 'all' ? ['daily/', 'weekly/', 'monthly/db/'] : [`${type === 'monthly' ? 'monthly/db/' : type + '/'}`];
   407	
   408	  for (const prefix of prefixes) {
   409	    console.log(`${prefix}`);
   410	    const backups = await listBackups(prefix);
   411	
   412	    if (backups.length === 0) {
   413	      console.log('  (empty)\n');
   414	      continue;
   415	    }
   416	
   417	    for (const backup of backups.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.LastModified) - new Date(a.LastModified))) {
   418	      const sizeKB = ((backup.Size || 0) / 1024).toFixed(2);
   419	      const date = backup.LastModified ? backup.LastModified.toISOString() : 'N/A';
   420	      console.log(`  ${backup.Key}`);
   421	      console.log(`  Size: ${sizeKB} KB | Modified: ${date}\n`);
   422	    }
   423	  }
   424	}
   425	
   426	async function main() {
   427	  const args = process.argv.slice(2);
   428	  const command = args[0] || 'help';
   429	
   430	  switch (command) {
   431	    case 'daily':
   432	      await runDailyBackup();
   433	      break;
   434	    case 'weekly':
   435	      await runWeeklyBackup();
   436	      break;
   437	    case 'monthly':
   438	      await runMonthlyBackup();
   439	      break;
   440	    case 'list':
   441	      await listExistingBackups(args[1]);
   442	      break;
   443	    case 'help':
   444	    default:
   445	      console.log('R2 Backup Script\n');
   446	      console.log('Usage:');
   447	      console.log('  node scripts/backup-to-r2.mjs daily');
   448	      console.log('  node scripts/backup-to-r2.mjs weekly');
   449	      console.log('  node scripts/backup-to-r2.mjs monthly');
   450	      console.log('  node scripts/backup-to-r2.mjs list [daily|weekly|monthly|all]\n');
   451	      console.log('Configure R2_BACKUP_BUCKET_NAME, R2_ACCOUNT_ID, R2_BACKUP_ACCESS_KEY_ID, and R2_BACKUP_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY.');
   452	      break;
   453	  }
   454	}
   455	
   456	main().catch((error) => {
   457	  console.error('Error:', error.message);
   458	  process.exit(1);

--- restore ---
     1	#!/usr/bin/env node
     2	
     3	/**
     4	 * Generic Cloudflare R2 restore helper.
     5	 *
     6	 * Required environment variables:
     7	 *   R2_BACKUP_BUCKET_NAME       - R2 bucket that stores backups
     8	 *   R2_ACCOUNT_ID               - Cloudflare account ID
     9	 *   R2_BACKUP_ACCESS_KEY_ID     - R2 access key for the backup bucket
    10	 *   R2_BACKUP_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY - R2 secret key for the backup bucket
    11	 *   GPG_PASSPHRASE              - Passphrase for encrypted backups
    12	 */
    13	
    14	import {
    15	  S3Client,
    16	  GetObjectCommand,
    17	  ListObjectsV2Command,
    18	} from '@aws-sdk/client-s3';
    19	import { NodeHttpHandler } from '@smithy/node-http-handler';
    20	import https from 'https';
    21	import fs from 'fs/promises';
    22	import path from 'path';
    23	import crypto from 'crypto';
    24	import zlib from 'zlib';
    25	
    26	function requireEnv(name) {
    27	  const value = process.env[name];
    28	  if (!value) {
    29	    throw new Error(`${name} environment variable is required`);
    30	  }
    31	  return value;
    32	}
    33	
    34	let configCache;
    35	let s3ClientCache;
    36	
    37	function getConfig() {
    38	  if (!configCache) {
    39	    configCache = {
    40	      bucketName: requireEnv('R2_BACKUP_BUCKET_NAME'),
    41	      accountId: requireEnv('R2_ACCOUNT_ID'),
    42	      accessKeyId: requireEnv('R2_BACKUP_ACCESS_KEY_ID'),
    43	      secretAccessKey: requireEnv('R2_BACKUP_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY'),
    44	    };
    45	  }
    46	
    47	  return configCache;
    48	}
    49	
    50	function getS3Client() {
    51	  if (!s3ClientCache) {
    52	    const config = getConfig();
    53	    s3ClientCache = new S3Client({
    54	      region: 'auto',
    55	      endpoint: `https://${config.accountId}.r2.cloudflarestorage.com`,
    56	      credentials: {
    57	        accessKeyId: config.accessKeyId,
    58	        secretAccessKey: config.secretAccessKey,
    59	      },
    60	      requestHandler: new NodeHttpHandler({
    61	        httpsAgent: new https.Agent({
    62	          keepAlive: true,
    63	          maxSockets: 50,
    64	        }),
    65	        requestTimeout: 60000,
    66	        connectionTimeout: 15000,
    67	      }),
    68	    });
    69	  }
    70	
    71	  return s3ClientCache;
    72	}
    73	
    74	function decryptData(encryptedData, passphrase) {
    75	  if (!passphrase) {
    76	    return zlib.gunzipSync(encryptedData);
    77	  }
    78	
    79	  const salt = encryptedData.subarray(0, 32);
    80	  const iv = encryptedData.subarray(32, 48);
    81	  const authTag = encryptedData.subarray(48, 64);
    82	  const encrypted = encryptedData.subarray(64);
    83	  const key = crypto.scryptSync(passphrase, salt, 32);
    84	
    85	  const decipher = crypto.createDecipheriv('aes-256-gcm', key, iv);
    86	  decipher.setAuthTag(authTag);
    87	
    88	  const decrypted = Buffer.concat([decipher.update(encrypted), decipher.final()]);
    89	  return zlib.gunzipSync(decrypted);
    90	}
    91	
    92	async function streamToBuffer(stream) {
    93	  const chunks = [];
    94	  for await (const chunk of stream) {
    95	    chunks.push(chunk);
    96	  }
    97	  return Buffer.concat(chunks);
    98	}
    99	
   100	async function listBackups(prefix = '') {
   101	  const config = getConfig();
   102	  const command = new ListObjectsV2Command({
   103	    Bucket: config.bucketName,
   104	    Prefix: prefix,
   105	  });
   106	
   107	  const response = await getS3Client().send(command);
   108	  return response.Contents || [];
   109	}
   110	
   111	async function downloadFromR2(key) {
   112	  const config = getConfig();
   113	  const command = new GetObjectCommand({
   114	    Bucket: config.bucketName,
   115	    Key: key,
   116	  });
   117	
   118	  const response = await getS3Client().send(command);
   119	  return streamToBuffer(response.Body);
   120	}
   121	
   122	async function listExistingBackups(type = 'all') {
   123	  const prefixes =
   124	    type === 'all' ? ['daily/', 'weekly/', 'monthly/db/'] : [`${type === 'monthly' ? 'monthly/db/' : type + '/'}`];
   125	
   126	  for (const prefix of prefixes) {
   127	    console.log(`${prefix}`);
   128	    const backups = await listBackups(prefix);
   129	
   130	    if (backups.length === 0) {
   131	      console.log('  (empty)\n');
   132	      continue;
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    for (const backup of backups.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.LastModified) - new Date(a.LastModified))) {
   136	      const sizeKB = ((backup.Size || 0) / 1024).toFixed(2);
   137	      const date = backup.LastModified ? backup.LastModified.toISOString() : 'N/A';
   138	      const encrypted = backup.Key.endsWith('.enc') ? ' encrypted' : '';
   139	      console.log(`  ${backup.Key}${encrypted}`);
   140	      console.log(`  Size: ${sizeKB} KB | Modified: ${date}\n`);
   141	    }
   142	  }
   143	}
   144	
   145	async function parseBackup(key) {
   146	  const rawData = await downloadFromR2(key);
   147	  const isEncrypted = key.endsWith('.enc');
   148	
   149	  if (isEncrypted && !process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE) {
   150	    throw new Error('GPG_PASSPHRASE environment variable required for encrypted backups');
   151	  }
   152	
   153	  const jsonData = decryptData(rawData, isEncrypted ? process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE : undefined).toString('utf-8');
   154	  return JSON.parse(jsonData);
   155	}
   156	
   157	async function downloadBackup(key, outputDir = './restore') {
   158	  console.log(`Downloading ${key}`);
   159	  console.log(`Output directory: ${outputDir}\n`);
   160	
   161	  const backupData = await parseBackup(key);
   162	
   163	  await fs.mkdir(outputDir, { recursive: true });
   164	
   165	  for (const [filePath, content] of Object.entries(backupData.files || {})) {
   166	    const fullPath = path.join(outputDir, filePath);
   167	    await fs.mkdir(path.dirname(fullPath), { recursive: true });
   168	    await fs.writeFile(fullPath, content, 'utf-8');
   169	    console.log(`Extracted ${filePath}`);
   170	  }
   171	
   172	  const metadataPath = path.join(outputDir, '_backup_metadata.json');
   173	  await fs.writeFile(
   174	    metadataPath,
   175	    JSON.stringify(
   176	      {
   177	        timestamp: backupData.timestamp,
   178	        type: backupData.type,
   179	        metadata: backupData.metadata,
   180	        restoredAt: new Date().toISOString(),
   181	        sourceKey: key,
   182	      },
   183	      null,
   184	      2
   185	    )
   186	  );
   187	
   188	  console.log('\nRestore completed successfully.');
   189	}
   190	
   191	async function verifyBackup(key) {
   192	  const backupData = await parseBackup(key);
   193	  const fileCount = Object.keys(backupData.files || {}).length;
   194	
   195	  console.log('Backup verification successful.');
   196	  console.log(`Type: ${backupData.type}`);
   197	  console.log(`Timestamp: ${backupData.timestamp}`);
   198	  console.log(`Files: ${fileCount}`);
   199	}
   200	
   201	async function main() {
   202	  const args = process.argv.slice(2);
   203	  const command = args[0] || 'help';
   204	
   205	  switch (command) {
   206	    case 'list':
   207	      await listExistingBackups(args[1]);
   208	      break;
   209	    case 'download':
   210	      if (!args[1]) {
   211	        throw new Error('Backup key required');
   212	      }
   213	      await downloadBackup(args[1], args[2] || './restore');
   214	      break;
   215	    case 'verify':
   216	      if (!args[1]) {
   217	        throw new Error('Backup key required');
   218	      }
   219	      await verifyBackup(args[1]);
   220	      break;
   221	    case 'help':
   222	    default:
   223	      console.log('R2 Restore Script\n');
   224	      console.log('Usage:');
   225	      console.log('  node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs list [daily|weekly|monthly|all]');
   226	      console.log('  node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs download <backup-key> [output-dir]');
   227	      console.log('  node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs verify <backup-key>');
   228	      break;
   229	  }
   230	}
   231	
   232	main().catch((error) => {
   233	  console.error('Error:', error.message);
   234	  process.exit(1);
   235	});

   102	/**
   103	 * Encrypt data using AES-256-GCM with passphrase
   104	 */
   105	function encryptData(data, passphrase) {
   106	  if (!passphrase) {
   107	    // If no passphrase, return gzipped data without encryption
   108	    return zlib.gzipSync(data);
   109	  }
   110	
   111	  // Derive key from passphrase using scrypt
   112	  const salt = crypto.randomBytes(32);
   113	  const key = crypto.scryptSync(passphrase, salt, 32);
   114	  const iv = crypto.randomBytes(16);
   115	
   116	  // Compress first, then encrypt
   117	  const compressed = zlib.gzipSync(data);
   118	
   119	  const cipher = crypto.createCipheriv('aes-256-gcm', key, iv);
   120	  const encrypted = Buffer.concat([cipher.update(compressed), cipher.final()]);
   121	  const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();
   122	
   123	  // Format: salt (32) + iv (16) + authTag (16) + encrypted data
   124	  return Buffer.concat([salt, iv, authTag, encrypted]);
   125	}
   126	
   127	/**
   128	 * Read file safely, return null if not exists
   129	 */
   130	async function readFileSafe(filePath) {
   131	  try {
   132	    return await fs.readFile(filePath, 'utf-8');
   133	  } catch {
   134	    return null;
   135	  }
   136	}
   137	
   138	/**
   139	 * Execute command safely, return null on error
   140	 */
   141	async function execSafe(command) {
   142	  try {
   143	    const { stdout } = await execAsync(command, { timeout: 30000 });
   144	    return stdout;
   145	  } catch {
   146	    return null;
   147	  }
   148	}
   149	
   150	/**
   151	 * Check if running on VPS
   152	 */
   153	function isVPS() {
   154	  return os.hostname() !== os.hostname().includes('dexter');
   155	}
   156	
   157	/**
   158	 * Get date string for backup naming
   159	 */
   160	function getDateString() {
   161	  const now = new Date();
   162	  return now.toISOString().split('T')[0]; // YYYY-MM-DD
   163	}
   164	
   165	/**
   166	 * Get week string for weekly backup naming
   167	 */
   168	function getWeekString() {
   169	  const now = new Date();
   170	  const year = now.getFullYear();
   171	  const weekNum = getWeekNumber(now);
   172	  return `${year}-W${weekNum.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
   173	}
   174	
   175	/**
   176	 * Get ISO week number
   177	 */
   178	function getWeekNumber(date) {
   179	  const d = new Date(Date.UTC(date.getFullYear(), date.getMonth(), date.getDate()));
   180	  const dayNum = d.getUTCDay() || 7;
   181	  d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + 4 - dayNum);
   182	  const yearStart = new Date(Date.UTC(d.getUTCFullYear(), 0, 1));
   183	  return Math.ceil(((d - yearStart) / 86400000 + 1) / 7);
   184	}
   185	
   186	/**
   187	 * Get month string for monthly backup naming
   188	 */
   189	function getMonthString() {
   190	  const now = new Date();
   191	  return `${now.getFullYear()}-${(now.getMonth() + 1).toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
   192	}
   193	
   194	/**
   195	 * Upload buffer to R2
   196	 */
   197	async function uploadToR2(key, data, metadata = {}) {
   198	  const command = new PutObjectCommand({
   199	    Bucket: CONFIG.bucketName,
   200	    Key: key,
   201	    Body: data,
   202	    ContentType: 'application/octet-stream',
   203	    Metadata: {
   204	      'backup-date': new Date().toISOString(),
   205	      ...metadata,
   206	    },
   207	  });
   208	
   209	  await s3Client.send(command);
   210	  return key;
   211	}
   212	
   213	/**
   214	 * List objects in R2 bucket with prefix
   215	 */
   216	async function listBackups(prefix) {
   217	  const command = new ListObjectsV2Command({
   218	    Bucket: CONFIG.bucketName,
   219	    Prefix: prefix,
   220	  });
   221	
   222	  const response = await s3Client.send(command);
   223	  return response.Contents || [];
   224	}
   225	
   226	/**
   227	 * Delete object from R2
   228	 */
   229	async function deleteFromR2(key) {
   230	  const command = new DeleteObjectCommand({
   231	    Bucket: CONFIG.bucketName,
   232	    Key: key,
   233	  });
   234	
   235	  await s3Client.send(command);
   236	}
   237	
   238	/**
   239	 * Cleanup old backups based on retention policy
   240	 */
   241	async function cleanupOldBackups(prefix, retentionCount) {
   242	  const backups = await listBackups(prefix);
   243	
   244	  if (backups.length <= retentionCount) {
   245	    console.log(`  ├─ Cleanup: ${backups.length} backups (within retention limit of ${retentionCount})`);
   246	    return;
   247	  }
   248	
   249	  // Sort by date (oldest first)
   250	  const sorted = backups.sort((a, b) => new Date(a.LastModified) - new Date(b.LastModified));
   251	
   252	  const toDelete = sorted.slice(0, sorted.length - retentionCount);
   253	
   254	  for (const backup of toDelete) {
   255	    console.log(`  ├─ Deleting old backup: ${backup.Key}`);
   256	    await deleteFromR2(backup.Key);
   257	  }
   258	
   259	  console.log(`  ├─ Cleaned up ${toDelete.length} old backups`);
   260	}
   261	
   262	/**
   263	 * Collect files for daily backup
   264	 */
   265	async function collectDailyBackupData() {
   266	  const backupData = {
   267	    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
   268	    type: 'daily',
   269	    files: {},
   270	    metadata: {
   271	      hostname: os.hostname(),
   272	      platform: os.platform(),
   273	      nodeVersion: process.version,
   274	    },
   275	  };
   276	
   277	  console.log('  ├─ Collecting environment files...');
   278	
   279	  // Try VPS paths first, fall back to local
   280	  const envProd = await readFileSafe(VPS_PATHS.envProd);
   281	  if (envProd) {
   282	    backupData.files['kitia.env'] = envProd;
   283	  } else {
   284	    // Try local .env
   285	    const localEnv = await readFileSafe(LOCAL_PATHS.envProd);
   286	    if (localEnv) {
   287	      backupData.files['kitia.env'] = localEnv;
   288	    }
   289	  }
   290	
   291	  const envStaging = await readFileSafe(VPS_PATHS.envStaging);
   292	  if (envStaging) {
   293	    backupData.files['kitia-staging.env'] = envStaging;
   294	  }
   295	
   296	  console.log('  ├─ Collecting nginx configurations...');
   297	
   298	  // Nginx configs
   299	  const nginxFiles = ['kitia.ir', 'staging.kitia.ir', 'logs.kitia.ir'];
   300	  for (const file of nginxFiles) {
   301	    const content = await readFileSafe(path.join(VPS_PATHS.nginxSitesAvailable, file));
   302	    if (content) {
   303	      backupData.files[`nginx/${file}`] = content;
   304	    }
   305	  }
   306	
   307	  const nginxConf = await readFileSafe(VPS_PATHS.nginxConf);
   308	  if (nginxConf) {
   309	    backupData.files['nginx/nginx.conf'] = nginxConf;
   310	  }
   311	
   312	  console.log('  ├─ Collecting htpasswd files...');
   313	
   314	  // htpasswd files
   315	  try {
   316	    const htpasswdOutput = await execSafe(`ls ${VPS_PATHS.htpasswd}/.htpasswd-* 2>/dev/null`);
   317	    if (htpasswdOutput) {
   318	      const files = htpasswdOutput.trim().split('\n').filter(Boolean);
   319	      for (const file of files) {
   320	        const content = await readFileSafe(file);
   321	        if (content) {
   322	          backupData.files[`htpasswd/${path.basename(file)}`] = content;
   323	        }
   324	      }
   325	    }
   326	  } catch {
   327	    // htpasswd files not found
   328	  }
   329	
   330	  console.log('  ├─ Collecting PM2 configuration...');
   331	
   332	  // PM2 config
   333	  const pm2Ecosystem =
   334	    (await readFileSafe(VPS_PATHS.pm2Ecosystem)) ||
   335	    (await readFileSafe(LOCAL_PATHS.pm2Ecosystem));
   336	  if (pm2Ecosystem) {
   337	    backupData.files['pm2/ecosystem.config.js'] = pm2Ecosystem;
   338	  }
   339	
   340	  const pm2Dump = await readFileSafe(VPS_PATHS.pm2Dump);
   341	  if (pm2Dump) {
   342	    backupData.files['pm2/dump.pm2'] = pm2Dump;
   343	  }
   344	
   345	  console.log('  ├─ Collecting SSH authorized keys...');
   346	
   347	  // SSH keys
   348	  const sshKeys = await readFileSafe(VPS_PATHS.sshKeys);
   349	  if (sshKeys) {
   350	    backupData.files['ssh/authorized_keys'] = sshKeys;
   351	  }
   352	
   353	  return backupData;
   354	}
   355	
   356	/**
   357	 * Collect files for weekly backup
   358	 */
   359	async function collectWeeklyBackupData() {
   360	  const backupData = {
   361	    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
   362	    type: 'weekly',
   363	    files: {},
   364	    metadata: {
   365	      hostname: os.hostname(),
   366	      platform: os.platform(),
   367	      nodeVersion: process.version,
   368	    },
   369	  };
   370	
   371	  console.log('  ├─ Collecting monitoring configurations...');
   372	
   373	  // Grafana config
   374	  const grafanaConfig = await readFileSafe(VPS_PATHS.grafanaConfig);
   375	  if (grafanaConfig) {
   376	    backupData.files['grafana/grafana.ini'] = grafanaConfig;
   377	  }
   378	
   379	  // Loki config
   380	  const lokiConfig = await readFileSafe(VPS_PATHS.lokiConfig);
   381	  if (lokiConfig) {
   382	    backupData.files['loki/config.yml'] = lokiConfig;
   383	  }
   384	
   385	  // Promtail config
   386	  const promtailConfig = await readFileSafe(VPS_PATHS.promtailConfig);
   387	  if (promtailConfig) {
   388	    backupData.files['promtail/config.yml'] = promtailConfig;
   389	  }
   390	
   391	  console.log('  ├─ Exporting Cloudflare DNS zone...');
   392	
   393	  // Cloudflare DNS export
   394	  const cfToken = process.env.CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN || process.env.CF_API_TOKEN;
   395	  const cfZoneId = process.env.CLOUDFLARE_ZONE_ID || '6ebecdc02622f961f532aa985cf6b851';
   396	
   397	  if (cfToken) {
   398	    try {
   399	      const response = await fetch(
   400	        `https://api.cloudflare.com/client/v4/zones/${cfZoneId}/dns_records/export`,
   401	        {
   402	          headers: {
   403	            Authorization: `Bearer ${cfToken}`,
   404	            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
   405	          },
   406	        }
   407	      );
   408	      if (response.ok) {
   409	        backupData.files['cloudflare/dns-zone.txt'] = await response.text();
   410	      }
   411	    } catch (error) {
   412	      console.log(`  │  └─ Warning: Could not export DNS zone: ${error.message}`);
   413	    }
   414	  } else {
   415	    console.log('  │  └─ Skipping DNS export (no CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN)');
   416	  }
   417	
   418	  console.log('  ├─ Collecting system state...');
   419	
   420	  // System state
   421	  const ufwRules = await execSafe('sudo ufw status verbose 2>/dev/null || echo "UFW not available"');
   422	  if (ufwRules) {
   423	    backupData.files['system/ufw-rules.txt'] = ufwRules;
   424	  }
   425	
   426	  const installedPackages = await execSafe('dpkg --get-selections 2>/dev/null || echo "dpkg not available"');
   427	  if (installedPackages) {
   428	    backupData.files['system/installed-packages.txt'] = installedPackages;
   429	  }
   430	
   431	  const enabledServices = await execSafe('systemctl list-unit-files --state=enabled 2>/dev/null || echo "systemctl not available"');
   432	  if (enabledServices) {
   433	    backupData.files['system/enabled-services.txt'] = enabledServices;
   434	  }
   435	
   436	  const crontab = await execSafe('crontab -l 2>/dev/null || echo "No crontab"');
   437	  if (crontab) {
   438	    backupData.files['system/crontab.txt'] = crontab;
   439	  }
   440	
   441	  const nodeVersion = await execSafe('node --version && npm --version');
   442	  if (nodeVersion) {
   443	    backupData.files['system/node-version.txt'] = nodeVersion;
   444	  }
   445	
   446	  return backupData;
   447	}
   448	
   449	/**
   450	 * Collect database backup data
   451	 */
   452	async function collectMonthlyDbBackupData() {
   453	  const backupData = {
   454	    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
   455	    type: 'monthly-db',
   456	    files: {},
   457	    metadata: {
   458	      hostname: os.hostname(),
   459	    },
   460	  };
   461	
   462	  const databaseUrl = process.env.DATABASE_URL;
   463	  if (!databaseUrl) {
   464	    throw new Error('DATABASE_URL environment variable not set');
   465	  }
   466	
   467	  console.log('  ├─ Exporting database...');
   468	
   469	  // Export database using pg_dump
   470	  const tmpDir = await fs.mkdtemp(path.join(os.tmpdir(), 'kitia-db-backup-'));
   471	  const dumpFile = path.join(tmpDir, 'database.sql');
   472	
   473	  // Use pg_dump 17 if available (for Supabase compatibility), otherwise fall back to system pg_dump
   474	  const pgDumpPath = await execSafe('test -f /usr/lib/postgresql/17/bin/pg_dump && echo "/usr/lib/postgresql/17/bin/pg_dump" || echo "pg_dump"');
   475	  const pgDump = (pgDumpPath || 'pg_dump').trim();
   476	
   477	  try {
   478	    // Use pg_dump to export database
   479	    await execAsync(`${pgDump} "${databaseUrl}" --no-owner --no-acl > "${dumpFile}"`, {
   480	      timeout: 300000, // 5 minutes
   481	    });
   482	
   483	    const dumpContent = await fs.readFile(dumpFile, 'utf-8');
   484	    backupData.files['database.sql'] = dumpContent;
   485	
   486	    console.log('  ├─ Exporting schema only...');
   487	
   488	    // Also export schema only
   489	    const schemaFile = path.join(tmpDir, 'schema.sql');
   490	    await execAsync(`${pgDump} "${databaseUrl}" --schema-only --no-owner --no-acl > "${schemaFile}"`, {
   491	      timeout: 300000, // 5 minutes (same as full dump)
   492	    });
   493	
   494	    const schemaContent = await fs.readFile(schemaFile, 'utf-8');
   495	    backupData.files['schema.sql'] = schemaContent;
   496	  } finally {
   497	    // Cleanup temp directory
   498	    await fs.rm(tmpDir, { recursive: true, force: true });
   499	  }
   500	
   501	  return backupData;
   502	}
   503	
   504	/**
   505	 * Run daily backup
   506	 */
   507	async function runDailyBackup() {
   508	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════');
   509	  console.log('  KITIA DAILY BACKUP');
   510	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n');
   511	
   512	  const dateStr = getDateString();
   513	  const backupKey = `daily/kitia-backup-${dateStr}.json.gz${process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE ? '.enc' : ''}`;
   514	
   515	  console.log(`📅 Date: ${dateStr}`);
   516	  console.log(`📁 Target: ${CONFIG.bucketName}/${backupKey}\n`);
   517	
   518	  try {
   519	    // Collect backup data
   520	    const backupData = await collectDailyBackupData();
   521	
   522	    const fileCount = Object.keys(backupData.files).length;
   523	    console.log(`  ├─ Collected ${fileCount} files\n`);
   524	
   525	    if (fileCount === 0) {
   526	      console.log('⚠️  No files collected for backup. Aborting.');
   527	      return;
   528	    }
   529	
   530	    // Serialize and encrypt
   531	    console.log('  ├─ Compressing and encrypting...');
   532	    const jsonData = JSON.stringify(backupData, null, 2);
   533	    const encrypted = encryptData(Buffer.from(jsonData), process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE);
   534	
   535	    // Upload to R2
   536	    console.log('  ├─ Uploading to R2...');
   537	    await uploadToR2(backupKey, encrypted, {
   538	      'file-count': fileCount.toString(),
   539	      encrypted: process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE ? 'true' : 'false',
   540	    });
   541	
   542	    console.log(`  ├─ Upload complete (${(encrypted.length / 1024).toFixed(2)} KB)\n`);
   543	
   544	    // Cleanup old backups
   545	    console.log('  ├─ Running cleanup...');
   546	    await cleanupOldBackups('daily/', CONFIG.retention.daily);
   547	
   548	    console.log('\n✅ Daily backup completed successfully!');
   549	    console.log(`📦 ${backupKey}`);
   550	  } catch (error) {
   551	    console.error('\n❌ Daily backup failed:', error.message);
   552	    throw error;
   553	  }
   554	
   555	  console.log('\n═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n');
   556	}
   557	
   558	/**
   559	 * Run weekly backup
   560	 */
   561	async function runWeeklyBackup() {
   562	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════');
   563	  console.log('  KITIA WEEKLY BACKUP');
   564	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n');
   565	
   566	  const weekStr = getWeekString();
   567	  const backupKey = `weekly/kitia-weekly-${weekStr}.json.gz${process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE ? '.enc' : ''}`;
   568	
   569	  console.log(`📅 Week: ${weekStr}`);
   570	  console.log(`📁 Target: ${CONFIG.bucketName}/${backupKey}\n`);
   571	
   572	  try {
   573	    // First run daily backup data collection
   574	    console.log('  ├─ Collecting daily backup data...');
   575	    const dailyData = await collectDailyBackupData();
   576	
   577	    // Then collect weekly-specific data
   578	    console.log('  ├─ Collecting weekly backup data...');
   579	    const weeklyData = await collectWeeklyBackupData();
   580	
   581	    // Merge data
   582	    const backupData = {
   583	      ...dailyData,
   584	      ...weeklyData,
   585	      type: 'weekly',
   586	      files: {
   587	        ...dailyData.files,
   588	        ...weeklyData.files,
   589	      },
   590	    };
   591	
   592	    const fileCount = Object.keys(backupData.files).length;
   593	    console.log(`  ├─ Collected ${fileCount} files\n`);
   594	
   595	    // Serialize and encrypt
   596	    console.log('  ├─ Compressing and encrypting...');
   597	    const jsonData = JSON.stringify(backupData, null, 2);
   598	    const encrypted = encryptData(Buffer.from(jsonData), process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE);
   599	
   600	    // Upload to R2
   601	    console.log('  ├─ Uploading to R2...');
   602	    await uploadToR2(backupKey, encrypted, {
   603	      'file-count': fileCount.toString(),
   604	      encrypted: process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE ? 'true' : 'false',
   605	    });
   606	
   607	    console.log(`  ├─ Upload complete (${(encrypted.length / 1024).toFixed(2)} KB)\n`);
   608	
   609	    // Cleanup old backups
   610	    console.log('  ├─ Running cleanup...');
   611	    await cleanupOldBackups('weekly/', CONFIG.retention.weekly);
   612	
   613	    console.log('\n✅ Weekly backup completed successfully!');
   614	    console.log(`📦 ${backupKey}`);
   615	  } catch (error) {
   616	    console.error('\n❌ Weekly backup failed:', error.message);
   617	    throw error;
   618	  }
   619	
   620	  console.log('\n═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n');
   621	}
   622

   626	async function runMonthlyBackup() {
   627	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════');
   628	  console.log('  KITIA MONTHLY DATABASE BACKUP');

   633

   635	  console.log(`📁 Target: ${CONFIG.bucketName}/${backupKey}\n`);

   639	    const backupData = await collectMonthlyDbBackupData();

   642	    console.log(`  ├─ Collected ${fileCount} files\n`);
   643

   645	    console.log('  ├─ Compressing and encrypting...');
   646	    const jsonData = JSON.stringify(backupData, null, 2);
   647	    const encrypted = encryptData(Buffer.from(jsonData), process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE);
   648	
   649	    // Upload to R2
   650	    console.log('  ├─ Uploading to R2...');
   651	    await uploadToR2(backupKey, encrypted, {
   652	      'file-count': fileCount.toString(),
   653	      encrypted: process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE ? 'true' : 'false',
   654	    });
   655	
   656	    console.log(`  ├─ Upload complete (${(encrypted.length / 1024).toFixed(2)} KB)\n`);
   657	
   658	    // Cleanup old backups

   660	    await cleanupOldBackups('monthly/db/', CONFIG.retention.monthly);
   661	
   662	    console.log('\n✅ Monthly database backup completed successfully!');
   663	    console.log(`📦 ${backupKey}`);
   664	  } catch (error) {
   665	    console.error('\n❌ Monthly database backup failed:', error.message);
   666	    throw error;
   667	  }
   668	
   669	  console.log('\n═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n');
   670	}
   671	
   672	/**
   673	 * List existing backups
   674	 */
   675	async function listExistingBackups(type = 'all') {
   676	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════');
   677	  console.log('  KITIA BACKUPS LIST');
   678	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n');
   679	
   680	  const prefixes = type === 'all' ? ['daily/', 'weekly/', 'monthly/db/'] : [`${type}/`];
   681	
   682	  for (const prefix of prefixes) {
   683	    console.log(`📁 ${prefix}`);
   684	    const backups = await listBackups(prefix);
   685	
   686	    if (backups.length === 0) {
   687	      console.log('   (empty)\n');
   688	      continue;
   689	    }
   690	
   691	    for (const backup of backups.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.LastModified) - new Date(a.LastModified))) {
   692	      const sizeKB = ((backup.Size || 0) / 1024).toFixed(2);
   693	      const date = backup.LastModified ? backup.LastModified.toISOString() : 'N/A';
   694	      console.log(`   ${backup.Key}`);
   695	      console.log(`   Size: ${sizeKB} KB | Modified: ${date}\n`);
   696	    }
   697	  }
   698	
   699	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n');
   700	}
   701	
   702	/**
   703	 * Main entry point
   704	 */
   705	async function main() {
   706	  const args = process.argv.slice(2);
   707	  const command = args[0] || 'help';
   708	
   709	  try {
   710	    switch (command) {
   711	      case 'daily':
   712	        await runDailyBackup();
   713	        break;
   714	
   715	      case 'weekly':
   716	        await runWeeklyBackup();
   717	        break;
   718	
   719	      case 'monthly':
   720	        await runMonthlyBackup();
   721	        break;
   722	
   723	      case 'list':
   724	        await listExistingBackups(args[1]);
   725	        break;
   726	
   727	      case 'help':
   728	      default:
   729	        console.log('Kitia Backup Script\n');
   730	        console.log('Usage:');
   731	        console.log('  node scripts/backup-to-r2.mjs daily    - Run daily backup');

     1	#!/usr/bin/env node

     3	/**
     4	 * Kitia Restore Script
     5	 *
     6	 * This script restores backups from Cloudflare R2.
     7	 *
     8	 * Usage:
     9	 *   List backups:  node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs list [daily|weekly|monthly]
    10	 *   Download:      node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs download <backup-key> [output-dir]
    11	 *   Verify:        node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs verify <backup-key>
    12	 *
    13	 * Required Environment Variables:
    14	 *   R2_BACKUP_ACCESS_KEY_ID     - R2 access key for backups bucket
    15	 *   R2_BACKUP_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY - R2 secret access key for backups bucket
    16	 *   R2_ACCOUNT_ID               - Cloudflare account ID
    17	 *   GPG_PASSPHRASE              - Passphrase for decryption (if backup is encrypted)

    65	/**
    66	 * Decrypt data using AES-256-GCM with passphrase
    67	 */
    68	function decryptData(encryptedData, passphrase) {
    69	  if (!passphrase) {
    70	    // If no passphrase, assume it's just gzipped
    71	    return zlib.gunzipSync(encryptedData);
    72	  }
    73	
    74	  // Format: salt (32) + iv (16) + authTag (16) + encrypted data
    75	  const salt = encryptedData.subarray(0, 32);
    76	  const iv = encryptedData.subarray(32, 48);
    77	  const authTag = encryptedData.subarray(48, 64);
    78	  const encrypted = encryptedData.subarray(64);
    79	
    80	  // Derive key from passphrase using scrypt
    81	  const key = crypto.scryptSync(passphrase, salt, 32);
    82	
    83	  const decipher = crypto.createDecipheriv('aes-256-gcm', key, iv);
    84	  decipher.setAuthTag(authTag);
    85	
    86	  const decrypted = Buffer.concat([decipher.update(encrypted), decipher.final()]);
    87	
    88	  // Decompress
    89	  return zlib.gunzipSync(decrypted);
    90	}
    91	
    92	/**
    93	 * Stream to buffer helper
    94	 */
    95	async function streamToBuffer(stream) {
    96	  const chunks = [];
    97	  for await (const chunk of stream) {
    98	    chunks.push(chunk);
    99	  }
   100	  return Buffer.concat(chunks);
   101	}

   103	/**
   104	 * List objects in R2 bucket with prefix
   105	 */
   106	async function listBackups(prefix = '') {
   107	  const command = new ListObjectsV2Command({
   108	    Bucket: CONFIG.bucketName,
   109	    Prefix: prefix,
   110	  });
   111	
   112	  const response = await s3Client.send(command);
   113	  return response.Contents || [];
   114	}

   116	/**
   117	 * Download object from R2
   118	 */
   119	async function downloadFromR2(key) {
   120	  const command = new GetObjectCommand({
   121	    Bucket: CONFIG.bucketName,
   122	    Key: key,
   123	  });
   124	
   125	  const response = await s3Client.send(command);
   126	  return streamToBuffer(response.Body);
   127	}

   129	/**
   130	 * List existing backups
   131	 */
   132	async function listExistingBackups(type = 'all') {
   133	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════');
   134	  console.log('  KITIA BACKUPS LIST');
   135	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n');
   136	
   137	  const prefixes =
   138	    type === 'all' ? ['daily/', 'weekly/', 'monthly/db/'] : [`${type === 'monthly' ? 'monthly/db/' : type + '/'}`];
   139	
   140	  for (const prefix of prefixes) {
   141	    console.log(`📁 ${prefix}`);
   142	    const backups = await listBackups(prefix);
   143	
   144	    if (backups.length === 0) {
   145	      console.log('   (empty)\n');
   146	      continue;
   147	    }
   148	
   149	    for (const backup of backups.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.LastModified) - new Date(a.LastModified))) {
   150	      const sizeKB = ((backup.Size || 0) / 1024).toFixed(2);
   151	      const date = backup.LastModified ? backup.LastModified.toISOString() : 'N/A';
   152	      const encrypted = backup.Key.endsWith('.enc') ? ' 🔒' : '';
   153	      console.log(`   ${backup.Key}${encrypted}`);
   154	      console.log(`   Size: ${sizeKB} KB | Modified: ${date}\n`);
   155	    }
   156	  }
   157	
   158	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n');
   159	}

   161	/**
   162	 * Download and extract backup
   163	 */
   164	async function downloadBackup(key, outputDir = './restore') {
   165	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════');
   166	  console.log('  KITIA BACKUP RESTORE');
   167	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n');
   168	
   169	  console.log(`📦 Downloading: ${key}`);
   170	  console.log(`📁 Output: ${outputDir}\n`);
   171	
   172	  try {
   173	    // Download from R2
   174	    console.log('  ├─ Downloading from R2...');
   175	    const encryptedData = await downloadFromR2(key);
   176	    console.log(`  ├─ Downloaded ${(encryptedData.length / 1024).toFixed(2)} KB`);
   177	
   178	    // Decrypt if needed
   179	    const isEncrypted = key.endsWith('.enc');
   180	    let jsonData;
   181	
   182	    if (isEncrypted) {
   183	      console.log('  ├─ Decrypting...');
   184	      if (!process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE) {
   185	        throw new Error('GPG_PASSPHRASE environment variable required for encrypted backups');
   186	      }
   187	      const decrypted = decryptData(encryptedData, process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE);
   188	      jsonData = decrypted.toString('utf-8');
   189	    } else {
   190	      console.log('  ├─ Decompressing...');
   191	      const decompressed = zlib.gunzipSync(encryptedData);
   192	      jsonData = decompressed.toString('utf-8');
   193	    }
   194	
   195	    // Parse backup data
   196	    console.log('  ├─ Parsing backup data...');
   197	    const backupData = JSON.parse(jsonData);
   198	
   199	    console.log(`  ├─ Backup type: ${backupData.type}`);
   200	    console.log(`  ├─ Backup date: ${backupData.timestamp}`);
   201	    console.log(`  ├─ Files: ${Object.keys(backupData.files).length}`);
   202	
   203	    // Create output directory
   204	    await fs.mkdir(outputDir, { recursive: true });
   205	
   206	    // Extract files
   207	    console.log('\n  ├─ Extracting files...');
   208	    for (const [filePath, content] of Object.entries(backupData.files)) {
   209	      const fullPath = path.join(outputDir, filePath);
   210	      const dir = path.dirname(fullPath);
   211	
   212	      await fs.mkdir(dir, { recursive: true });
   213	      await fs.writeFile(fullPath, content, 'utf-8');
   214	      console.log(`  │  └─ ${filePath}`);
   215	    }
   216	
   217	    // Write metadata
   218	    const metadataPath = path.join(outputDir, '_backup_metadata.json');
   219	    await fs.writeFile(
   220	      metadataPath,
   221	      JSON.stringify(
   222	        {
   223	          timestamp: backupData.timestamp,
   224	          type: backupData.type,
   225	          metadata: backupData.metadata,
   226	          restoredAt: new Date().toISOString(),
   227	          sourceKey: key,
   228	        },
   229	        null,
   230	        2
   231	      )
   232	    );
   233	
   234	    console.log('\n✅ Restore completed successfully!');
   235	    console.log(`📁 Files extracted to: ${path.resolve(outputDir)}`);
   236	  } catch (error) {
   237	    console.error('\n❌ Restore failed:', error.message);
   238	    throw error;
   239	  }
   240	
   241	  console.log('\n═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n');
   242	}
   243	
   244	/**
   245	 * Verify backup integrity
   246	 */
   247	async function verifyBackup(key) {
   248	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════');
   249	  console.log('  KITIA BACKUP VERIFICATION');
   250	  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n');
   251	
   252	  console.log(`📦 Verifying: ${key}\n`);
   253	
   254	  try {
   255	    // Download from R2
   256	    console.log('  ├─ Downloading from R2...');
   257	    const encryptedData = await downloadFromR2(key);
   258	    console.log(`  ├─ Downloaded ${(encryptedData.length / 1024).toFixed(2)} KB`);
   259	
   260	    // Decrypt if needed
   261	    const isEncrypted = key.endsWith('.enc');
   262	    let jsonData;
   263	
   264	    if (isEncrypted) {
   265	      console.log('  ├─ Decrypting...');
   266	      if (!process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE) {
   267	        throw new Error('GPG_PASSPHRASE environment variable required for encrypted backups');
   268	      }
   269	      const decrypted = decryptData(encryptedData, process.env.GPG_PASSPHRASE);
   270	      jsonData = decrypted.toString('utf-8');
   271	    } else {
   272	      console.log('  ├─ Decompressing...');
   273	      const decompressed = zlib.gunzipSync(encryptedData);
   274	      jsonData = decompressed.toString('utf-8');
   275	    }
   276	
   277	    // Parse and validate
   278	    console.log('  ├─ Parsing backup data...');
   279	    const backupData = JSON.parse(jsonData);
   280	
   281	    console.log('\n📋 Backup Details:');
   282	    console.log(`   Type: ${backupData.type}`);
   283	    console.log(`   Timestamp: ${backupData.timestamp}`);
   284	    console.log(`   Hostname: ${backupData.metadata?.hostname || 'N/A'}`);
   285	    console.log(`   Platform: ${backupData.metadata?.platform || 'N/A'}`);
   286	    console.log(`   Node Version: ${backupData.metadata?.nodeVersion || 'N/A'}`);
   287	
   288	    console.log('\n📁 Files Included:');
   289	    for (const [filePath, content] of Object.entries(backupData.files)) {
   290	      const sizeKB = (Buffer.byteLength(content, 'utf-8') / 1024).toFixed(2);
   291	      console.log(`   ${filePath} (${sizeKB} KB)`);
   292	    }
   293	
   294	    console.log('\n✅ Backup verification successful!');
   295	    console.log('   All data is readable and properly formatted.');
   296	  } catch (error) {
   297	    console.error('\n❌ Verification failed:', error.message);
   298	    throw error;
   299	  }
   300	
   301	  console.log('\n═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n');
   302	}
   303	
   304	/**
   305	 * Main entry point
   306	 */
   307	async function main() {
   308	  const args = process.argv.slice(2);
   309	  const command = args[0] || 'help';
   310	
   311	  try {
   312	    switch (command) {
   313	      case 'list':
   314	        await listExistingBackups(args[1]);
   315	        break;
   316	
   317	      case 'download':
   318	        if (!args[1]) {
   319	          console.error('Error: Backup key required');
   320	          console.log('Usage: node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs download <backup-key> [output-dir]');
   321	          process.exit(1);
   322	        }
   323	        await downloadBackup(args[1], args[2] || './restore');
   324	        break;
   325	
   326	      case 'verify':
   327	        if (!args[1]) {
   328	          console.error('Error: Backup key required');
   329	          console.log('Usage: node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs verify <backup-key>');
   330	          process.exit(1);
   331	        }
   332	        await verifyBackup(args[1]);
   333	        break;
   334	
   335	      case 'help':
   336	      default:
   337	        console.log('Kitia Restore Script\n');
   338	        console.log('Usage:');
   339	        console.log('  node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs list [type]           - List backups (daily|weekly|monthly|all)');
   340	        console.log('  node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs download <key> [dir]  - Download and extract backup');
   341	        console.log('  node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs verify <key>          - Verify backup integrity\n');
   342	        console.log('Environment Variables:');
   343	        console.log('  GPG_PASSPHRASE  - Passphrase for decryption (required for encrypted backups)\n');
   344	        console.log('Examples:');
   345	        console.log('  node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs list daily');
   346	        console.log('  node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs download daily/kitia-backup-2025-01-15.json.gz.enc ./restore');
   347	        console.log('  node scripts/restore-from-r2.mjs verify weekly/kitia-weekly-2025-W03.json.gz.enc');
   348	        break;
   349	    }
   350	  } catch (error) {
   351	    console.error('Error:', error.message);
   352	    process.exit(1);
   353	  }
   354	}
   355	
   356	main();

- `src/components/profile/ProfileEditForm.tsx`
- `src/lib/email/client.ts`
- `tests/unit/utils/persian.test.ts`

## Requirements

- Replace Persian visible UI strings with concise English defaults.
- Replace API error messages with English messages that are safe to expose.
- Replace auth credential labels and errors with neutral English labels.

- Keep RTL support through direction config, not Persian content.
